            b1[i].setAttribute("class", "vm-placement");
            b1[i].setAttribute("data-id", "6017d58cfe24b76bfed2654b");
            if (i==0) b1[i].setAttribute("data-display-type", "hybrid-banner");
          }
          window.top.__vm_add.push(b1[i]);
        }

        for (let i=0;i<b2.length;i++) {
          if (window.innerWidth < 728) {
            b2[i].setAttribute("class", "vm-placement");
            b2[i].setAttribute("data-id", "6017d5c235df310fc2d5f18d");
            if (i==0) b2[i].setAttribute("data-display-type", "hybrid-banner");
          } else if (window.innerWidth < 970) {
            b2[i].setAttribute("class", "vm-placement");
            b2[i].setAttribute("data-id", "6017d583f3cede114f2df84c");
          } else {
            b2[i].setAttribute("class", "vm-placement");
            b2[i].setAttribute("data-id", "6017d58cfe24b76bfed2654b");
          }
          window.top.__vm_add.push(b2[i]);
        }

        for (let i=0;i<b3.length;i++) {
          if (window.innerWidth < 728) {
            b3[i].setAttribute("class", "vm-placement");

<script type="text/javascript" defer>
if ('serviceWorker' in navigator) {
  navigator.serviceWorker.register('https://brawlify.com/cache.js');
}
function setCookie(cname, cvalue, exdays) {
    let d = new Date();
    d.setTime(d.getTime() + (exdays * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000));
    let expires = "expires="+d.toUTCString();
    document.cookie = cname + "=" + cvalue + ";" + expires + ";path=/";
}

function getCookie(cname) {
    let name = cname + "=";
    let ca = document.cookie.split(';');
    for(let i = 0; i < ca.length; i++) {
      let c = ca[i];
      while (c.charAt(0) == ' ') {
        c = c.substring(1);
      }
      if (c.indexOf(name) == 0) {
        return c.substring(name.length, c.length);
      }
    }
    return false;
}

// Language Set
function setPrimaryPageLanguage(lang) {
    localStorage.setItem("langData", JSON.stringify({ lang: lang, path: ((lang=='en')?'':'/'+lang), fixed: true, lastChanged:moment(new Date())}));
}

// Language Switcher
function pageLangChecker() {
    var pageLang = localStorage.getItem("langData");
    if (!pageLang) return;
    pageLang = JSON.parse(pageLang);
    if (window.location.pathname !== pageLang.path+noLangVersion) window.location.pathname = pageLang.path+noLangVersion;
    if (pageLang.fixed == false) {
        var setIntVal1 = false;
        function setLangInternal() {
            if (typeof setPrimaryPageLanguage === "function") {
                if (setIntVal1 == false) {
                    setPrimaryPageLanguage(pageLang.lang);
                    setIntVal1 = true;
                }
                return true;
            } else return false;
        }
        var langIntervalChecker = setInterval(function() { 
            if (setLangInternal() == true) clearInterval(langIntervalChecker);
        }, 1000);
    }
}
pageLangChecker();

// Language Notificator
function pageLangSetup() {
    var pageLang = localStorage.getItem("langData");
    if (!pageLang) {
        var lang = ((window.navigator.languages)?window.navigator.languages[0]:null)||window.navigator.language||window.navigator.browserLanguage||window.navigator.userLanguage;
        if (!lang) return;
        lang = ((lang=='pt-br'||lang==='pt_br')?'br':((lang.indexOf('Hans')!==-1)?'cn':((lang.indexOf('Hant')!==-1)?'zh':((lang.slice(0,2)=='cs')?'cz':((lang.indexOf('-')!==-1)?lang.split('-')[0]:((lang.indexOf('_')!==-1)?lang.split('_')[0]:lang)))))).slice(0,2);
        if (lang == 'en') return localStorage.setItem("langData", JSON.stringify({ lang:'en',path:'',fixed:true,lastChanged:moment(new Date())}));
        var langNotif = document.getElementById('langNotification-'+lang);
        if (langNotif) {
            pageLang = { lang: lang, path: ((lang=='en')?'':'/'+lang), fixed: false, lastChanged:moment(new Date())};
            localStorage.setItem("langData", JSON.stringify(pageLang));
            if (window.location.pathname !== pageLang.path+noLangVersion) window.location.pathname = pageLang.path+noLangVersion;
            else langNotif.style.display = 'block';
        }
    } else {
        pageLang = JSON.parse(pageLang);
        if (pageLang.fixed == false) {
            var langNotif = document.getElementById('langNotification-'+pageLang.lang);
            if (langNotif) langNotif.style.display = 'block';
        }
    }
}
pageLangSetup();

function checkPwa() {
    var pwaData = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem("pwaData"));
    if (pwaData && pwaData.hasPwa == true) return true;
    return false;
}

function checkSupport() {
    var supportData = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem("supportData"));
    if (supportData && supportData.supported == true && moment().diff(moment(supportData.lastTime), 'days') < 7) return true;
    return false;
}

// Check if user is Premium
function checkPremium() {
    var premiumUser = ((getCookie('premiumUser'))?getCookie('premiumUser'):false);
    if (premiumUser) return true;
    else {
      var premiumStorageFallback = localStorage.getItem("premiumStorageFallback");
      if (premiumStorageFallback) premiumStorageFallback = JSON.parse(premiumStorageFallback);
      if (premiumStorageFallback && premiumStorageFallback.tag) {
        setCookie("premiumUser", premiumStorageFallback.tag, 3);
        localStorage.removeItem("premiumUserLastCheck");
        location.reload();
        return true;
      }
    }
    return false;
}

// Check for excludability
function checkExcludability() {
    if (checkPremium() == true) return true;
    return excludedFromLoading;
}

function apiFetch(path, auth = true) {
    return new Promise(async resolve => {
        var xhr = new XMLHttpRequest();
        xhr.open('GET', 'https://api.brawlapi.com/'+path, true);
        if (auth && apiKey) xhr.setRequestHeader('Authorization', apiKey);
        xhr.timeout = 15000;
        xhr.send();
        xhr.onreadystatechange = processRequest;
        function processRequest(e) {
            if (xhr.readyState == 4 && xhr.status == 200) {
                try {
                    var response = JSON.parse(xhr.responseText);
                    response.statusCode = xhr.status;
                    if (response && response.error !== true) {
                        // Valid response
                        return resolve(response);
                    } else {
                        // Failed to get data. Invalid server response!;
                        return resolve(response);
                    }
                } catch (e) {
                    return resolve({status:'err',statusCode:1});
                }
            } else if (xhr.readyState == 4) {
                // Failed to get data. Check your internet connection!;
                return resolve({status:'err',statusCode:0});
            }
        }
    });
}

function getStrings(lang = 'en') {
    return new Promise(async resolve => {
        let data = await apiFetch('v1/translations/'+lang, false);
        return resolve(data);
    });
}

// Load strings
async function loadStrings() {
    var b_s = localStorage.getItem("locale_strings");
    if (b_s) {
        var backup_strings = JSON.parse(b_s);
        if (backup_strings) {
            strings = backup_strings;
            if (backup_strings['fetch_time'] && Date.now() - backup_strings['fetch_time'] < 86400000) return strings;
        }
    }
    var stringData = await getStrings(lang);
    if (stringData && stringData.hasOwnProperty('statusCode') && stringData.statusCode == 200) {
        stringData.strings['fetch_time'] = Date.now();
        localStorage.setItem("locale_strings", JSON.stringify(stringData.strings));
        strings = stringData.strings;
        return stringData.strings;
    } else {
        if (b_s) {
            strings = JSON.parse(b_s);
            return strings;
        } else return {};
    };
}
loadStrings();

function extendPremiumCookie() {
  var pc = getCookie('premiumUser');
  if (!pc) return;
  if (pc.includes('{')) {
    pc = JSON.parse(pc);
    setCookie("premiumUser", pc.tag, 7);
    pc = getCookie('premiumUser');
  }

  var premiumUserLastCheck = localStorage.getItem("premiumUserLastCheck");
  if (!premiumUserLastCheck || (Date.now()-premiumUserLastCheck) >= 1800000) {
    localStorage.setItem("premiumUserLastCheck", Date.now());

    var xhr = new XMLHttpRequest();
    xhr.open('GET', 'https://api.brawlify.com/v1/subscriptions/'+pc, true);
    xhr.timeout = 15000;
    xhr.send();
    xhr.onreadystatechange = processRequest;
    function processRequest(e) {
      if (xhr.readyState == 4) {
        var response = JSON.parse(xhr.responseText);
        if (xhr.status == 200 && response && response.status && response.status == 'active') {
          localStorage.setItem("premiumStorageFallback", JSON.stringify({tag:response.tag}));
          setCookie("premiumUser", response.tag, 30);
        } else {
          setCookie("premiumUser", '', -365);
          localStorage.removeItem("premiumStorageFallback");
          localStorage.removeItem("premiumUserLastCheck");
          location.reload();
        }
      }
    }
  }
}

function makeTemporaryUserID(length) {
  var result           = '';
  var characters       = 'ABCDEFGHIJKLMNOPQRSTUVWXYZabcdefghijklmnopqrstuvwxyz0123456789';
  var charactersLength = characters.length;
  for ( var i = 0; i < length; i++ ) {
      result += characters.charAt(Math.floor(Math.random() * charactersLength));
  }
  return result;
}

function playVideoAd(purpose, userId) {
  if (typeof ramp == 'undefined' || typeof ramp.showRewardedVideo !== 'function') {
    document.getElementById('premiumStringItem').style.display = 'none';
    if (document.getElementById('watchAdForRewardBtn')) document.getElementById('watchAdForRewardBtn').classList.add('d-none');
    return alert('You may be blocking ads with an Ad Block or there\'s currently no video for you available.\n\nPlease disable ad block or try again later!');
  }
  if (purpose == 'removeAds' && userId == null) {
    userId = makeTemporaryUserID(10);
    if (confirm('Would you like to remove ads for free temporarily?\n\nWe will play an ad for you to watch to remove ads!') == true) {
      var xhr = new XMLHttpRequest();
      xhr.open('GET', 'https://api.brawlify.com/v1/rewarded-video/init/'+userId, true);
      xhr.timeout = 15000;
      xhr.send();
      xhr.onreadystatechange = processRequest;
      function processRequest(e) {
        if (xhr.readyState == 4 && xhr.status == 200) {
          try {
            var response = JSON.parse(xhr.responseText);
            if (response.code) {
              ramp.showRewardedVideo({
                code: response.code,
                userId: userId,
                callback:(response) => {
                  if (response.rewardUser == true) {
                    var xhr = new XMLHttpRequest();
                    xhr.open('GET', 'https://api.brawlify.com/v1/rewarded-video/verify/'+userId+'/'+response.code, true);
                    xhr.timeout = 15000;
                    xhr.send();
                    xhr.onreadystatechange = processRequest;
                    function processRequest(e) {
                      if (xhr.readyState == 4 && xhr.status == 200) {
                        try {
                          var responseVer = JSON.parse(xhr.responseText);
                          if (responseVer.status == 'success') {
                            let d = new Date();
                            d.setTime(d.getTime() + (((response.adPlayed==true&&response.adType=='video')?2:1) * 60 * 60 * 1000));
                            let expires = "expires="+d.toUTCString();
                            document.cookie = "premiumUser=VIDEOADS;" + expires + ";path=/";
                            localStorage.setItem("premiumUserLastCheck", (Date.now()+((response.adPlayed==true&&response.adType=='video')?7200000:3600000)));
                            if (response.adPlayed == true && response.adType=='video') alert('Thank you for watching the video ad!\n\nYou got removed ads for two hours!');
                            else if (response.adPlayed == true) alert('Thank you, we couldn\'t find a video ad for you but you still get half the reward.\n\nYou got removed ads for one hour!');
                            else alert('Thank you, the video ad didn\'t play but you got half the reward.\n\nYou got removed ads for one hour!');
                            return location.reload();
                          } else {
                            return alert('Something went wrong, we couldn\'t verify that you watched the ad.\nTry again later, please.');
                          }
                        } catch (e) {
                          return alert('Something went wrong, we couldn\'t verify that you watched the ad.\nTry again later, please.');
                        }
                      } else if (xhr.readyState == 4) {
                        return alert('Something went wrong, we couldn\'t verify that you watched the ad.\nTry again later, please.');
                      }
                    }
                  } else {
                    document.getElementById('premiumStringItem').style.display = 'none';
                    if (document.getElementById('watchAdForRewardBtn')) document.getElementById('watchAdForRewardBtn').classList.add('d-none');
                    return alert('Hmm, seems like this time you weren\'t eligible. Try it again later.');
                  }
                }
              });
            } else {
              return alert('Something went wrong, we couldn\'t play a video ad for you right now.\nTry again later, please.');
            }
          } catch (e) {
            return alert('Something went wrong, we couldn\'t play a video ad for you right now.\nTry again later, please.');
          }
        } else if (xhr.readyState == 4) {
          return alert('Something went wrong, we couldn\'t play a video ad for you right now.\nTry again later, please.');
        }
      }
    }
  } else if (purpose.startsWith('tracker') && typeof userId == 'string') {
    var xhr = new XMLHttpRequest();
    xhr.open('GET', 'https://api.brawlify.com/v1/rewarded-video/init/'+((purpose.toLowerCase().includes('player'))?'player':'club')+'-'+userId.replace('#',''), true);
    xhr.timeout = 15000;
    xhr.send();
    xhr.onreadystatechange = processRequest;
    function processRequest(e) {
      if (xhr.readyState == 4 && xhr.status == 200) {
        try {
          var response = JSON.parse(xhr.responseText);
          if (response.code) {
            ramp.showRewardedVideo({
              code: response.code,
              userId: userId,
              callback:(response) => {
                if (response.rewardUser == true) {
                  var xhr = new XMLHttpRequest();
                  xhr.open('GET', 'https://api.brawlify.com/v1/rewarded-video/verify/'+((purpose.toLowerCase().includes('player'))?'player':'club')+'-'+userId.replace('#','')+'/'+response.code, true);
                  xhr.timeout = 15000;
                  xhr.send();
                  xhr.onreadystatechange = processRequest;
                  function processRequest(e) {
                    if (xhr.readyState == 4 && xhr.status == 200) {
                      try {
                        var responseVer = JSON.parse(xhr.responseText);
                        if (responseVer.status == 'success') {
                          alert('Thank you for watching the video ad!\n\n'+((purpose.toLowerCase().includes('player'))?'This profile will be actively monitored for the next 3 days and we will track changes on graphs & in logs.':'This club will be actively monitored for the next 5 days and we will track changes on graphs & in logs.'));
                          document.getElementById('premiumStringItem').style.display = 'none';
                          if (document.getElementById('watchAdForRewardBtn')) document.getElementById('watchAdForRewardBtn').classList.add('d-none');
                        } else {
                          return alert('Something went wrong, we couldn\'t verify that you watched the ad.\nTry again later, please.');
                        }
                      } catch (e) {
                        return alert('Something went wrong, we couldn\'t verify that you watched the ad.\nTry again later, please.');
                      }
                    } else if (xhr.readyState == 4) {
                      return alert('Something went wrong, we couldn\'t verify that you watched the ad.\nTry again later, please.');
                    }
                  }
                } else {
                  document.getElementById('premiumStringItem').style.display = 'none';
                  if (document.getElementById('watchAdForRewardBtn')) document.getElementById('watchAdForRewardBtn').classList.add('d-none');
                  return alert('Hmm, seems like this time you weren\'t eligible. Try it again later.');
                }
              }
            });
          } else {
            return alert('Something went wrong, we couldn\'t play a video ad for you right now.\nTry again later, please.');
          }
        } catch (e) {
          return alert('Something went wrong, we couldn\'t play a video ad for you right now.\nTry again later, please.');
        }
      } else if (xhr.readyState == 4) {
        return alert('Something went wrong, we couldn\'t play a video ad for you right now.\nTry again later, please.');
      }
    }
  } else {
    return alert('Something went wrong, please try again later.');
  }
}

if (checkPremium() == true) extendPremiumCookie();

    }
}

        legend: {
          onClick: function (e, legendItem, legend) {
            if (!legend.chart.isDatasetVisible(legendItem.datasetIndex)) {
              legend.chart.show(legendItem.datasetIndex);
              for (let i=0;i<legend.chart.data.datasets.length;i++) if (i !== legendItem.datasetIndex) legend.chart.hide(i);
              legend.chart.config.data.labels = legend.chart.data.datasets[legendItem.datasetIndex].labels;
              let curr = userSummary[legend.chart.data.datasets[legendItem.datasetIndex].labelRaw];
              document.getElementById('mainRecent').classList.remove('text-success', 'text-warning', 'text-danger');
              document.getElementById('mainDaily').classList.remove('text-success', 'text-warning', 'text-danger');
              document.getElementById('mainWeekly').classList.remove('text-success', 'text-warning', 'text-danger');
              document.getElementById('mainSeason').classList.remove('text-success', 'text-warning', 'text-danger');

              document.getElementById('mainRecent').innerHTML = ((curr.recent>0)?'+'+curr.recent.toLocaleString(lang):((curr.recent<0)?curr.recent.toLocaleString(lang):'+0'));
              document.getElementById('mainDaily').innerHTML = ((curr.today>0)?'+'+curr.today.toLocaleString(lang):((curr.today<0)?curr.today.toLocaleString(lang):'+0'));
              document.getElementById('mainWeekly').innerHTML = ((curr.week>0)?'+'+curr.week.toLocaleString(lang):((curr.week<0)?curr.week.toLocaleString(lang):'+0'));
              document.getElementById('mainSeason').innerHTML = ((curr.season>0)?'+'+curr.season.toLocaleString(lang):((curr.season<0)?curr.season.toLocaleString(lang):'+0'));

              document.getElementById('mainRecent').classList.add(((curr.recent>0)?'text-success':((curr.recent<0)?'text-danger':'text-warning')));
              document.getElementById('mainDaily').classList.add(((curr.today>0)?'text-success':((curr.today<0)?'text-danger':'text-warning')));
              document.getElementById('mainWeekly').classList.add(((curr.week>0)?'text-success':((curr.week<0)?'text-danger':'text-warning')));
              document.getElementById('mainSeason').classList.add(((curr.season>0)?'text-success':((curr.season<0)?'text-danger':'text-warning')));

              legend.chart.update();
            }
          }
        }
      }
    }
  });

  document.getElementById('progressionGraphsLoader').style.display = "none";

  function switchGraphGrouping() {
    dailyGraphGrouping = !dailyGraphGrouping;
    document.getElementById('graphGroupingBtn').innerHTML = ((dailyGraphGrouping)?'Graph: Daily':'Graph: All');

    let tgi = 0;
    for (let i=0;i<((dailyGraphGrouping)?dailyProgressionGraphDatasets:progressionGraphDatasets).length;i++) {
      if (((dailyGraphGrouping)?dailyProgressionGraphDatasets:progressionGraphDatasets)[i]['labelRaw'] == 'trophies') tgi = i;
    }

    progressionGraph.config.data.labels = ((dailyGraphGrouping)?dailyProgressionGraphDatasets[Object.keys(dailyProgressionGraphDatasets)[tgi]]['labels']:progressionGraphDatasets[Object.keys(dailyProgressionGraphDatasets)[tgi]]['labels']);
    progressionGraph.config.data.datasets = ((dailyGraphGrouping)?dailyProgressionGraphDatasets:progressionGraphDatasets);
    progressionGraph.update();

    let bIds = Object.keys(progressionGraphs);
    for (let i=0;i<bIds.length;i++) {
      let currentLabelsUpdated = [];
      let brawlerDataUpdated = ((dailyGraphGrouping)?dailyBrawlerGraphDatasets[bIds[i]]:brawlerGraphDatasets[bIds[i]]);
      for (let i=0;i<brawlerDataUpdated.length;i++) {
        if (brawlerDataUpdated[i].labelRaw == 'trophies') currentLabelsUpdated = brawlerDataUpdated[i].labels;
      }

      progressionGraphs[bIds[i]].config.data.labels = currentLabelsUpdated;
      progressionGraphs[bIds[i]].config.data.datasets = brawlerDataUpdated;
      progressionGraphs[bIds[i]].update();
    }  
  }

let initStatus = {};
function initBrawlerBlock(id) {
  if (initStatus[id]) return;
  initStatus[id] = true;

  progressionGraphDoc = document.getElementById('progression-graph-'+id);
  let currentLabels = [];
  let brawlerData = ((dailyGraphGrouping)?dailyBrawlerGraphDatasets[id]:brawlerGraphDatasets[id]);
  if (brawlerData && brawlerData.length) {
    for (let i=0;i<brawlerData.length;i++) {
      if (brawlerData[i].labelRaw == 'trophies') currentLabels = brawlerData[i].labels;
    }
  }

  if (currentLabels.length > 1) {
    progressionGraphs[id] = new Chart(progressionGraphDoc, {
      type: 'line',
      data: {
        labels: currentLabels,
        datasets: brawlerData
      },
      options: {
        responsive:true,
        maintainAspectRatio: false,
        normalized: true,
        animation: false,
        plugins: {
          legend: {
            onClick: function (e, legendItem, legend) {
              if (!legend.chart.isDatasetVisible(legendItem.datasetIndex)) {
                legend.chart.show(legendItem.datasetIndex);
                for (let i=0;i<legend.chart.data.datasets.length;i++) if (i !== legendItem.datasetIndex) legend.chart.hide(i);
                legend.chart.config.data.labels = legend.chart.data.datasets[legendItem.datasetIndex].labels;
                const brawlerId = id;
                let curr = brawlerSummary[brawlerId][legend.chart.data.datasets[legendItem.datasetIndex].labelRaw];
                document.getElementById('sideRecent-'+brawlerId).classList.remove('text-success', 'text-warning', 'text-danger');
                document.getElementById('sideDaily-'+brawlerId).classList.remove('text-success', 'text-warning', 'text-danger');
                document.getElementById('sideWeekly-'+brawlerId).classList.remove('text-success', 'text-warning', 'text-danger');
                document.getElementById('sideHistory-'+brawlerId).classList.remove('text-success', 'text-warning', 'text-danger');

                document.getElementById('sideRecent-'+brawlerId).innerHTML = ((curr.recent>0)?'+'+curr.recent.toLocaleString(lang):((curr.recent<0)?curr.recent.toLocaleString(lang):'+0'));
                document.getElementById('sideDaily-'+brawlerId).innerHTML = ((curr.today>0)?'+'+curr.today.toLocaleString(lang):((curr.today<0)?curr.today.toLocaleString(lang):'+0'));
                document.getElementById('sideWeekly-'+brawlerId).innerHTML = ((curr.week>0)?'+'+curr.week.toLocaleString(lang):((curr.week<0)?curr.week.toLocaleString(lang):'+0'));
                document.getElementById('sideHistory-'+brawlerId).innerHTML = ((curr.season>0)?'+'+curr.season.toLocaleString(lang):((curr.season<0)?curr.season.toLocaleString(lang):'+0'));

                document.getElementById('sideRecent-'+brawlerId).classList.add(((curr.recent>0)?'text-success':((curr.recent<0)?'text-danger':'text-warning')));
                document.getElementById('sideDaily-'+brawlerId).classList.add(((curr.today>0)?'text-success':((curr.today<0)?'text-danger':'text-warning')));
                document.getElementById('sideWeekly-'+brawlerId).classList.add(((curr.week>0)?'text-success':((curr.week<0)?'text-danger':'text-warning')));
                document.getElementById('sideHistory-'+brawlerId).classList.add(((curr.season>0)?'text-success':((curr.season<0)?'text-danger':'text-warning')));

                legend.chart.update();
              }
            }
          }
        }
      }
    });
    progressionGraphDoc.style.display = null;
    document.getElementById('progressionGraphsLoader-'+id).style.display = "none";
  } else {
    progressionGraphDoc.style.display = "none";
    document.getElementById('progressionGraphsLoader-'+id).style.display = "none";
    document.getElementById('mainError-'+id).style.display = null;
    document.getElementById('mainErrorText-'+id).innerHTML = "Not enough data for graphs.<br>Please check back later and often so we can collect more data!";
  }
}

  document.getElementById('brawlerSelect1').addEventListener('change', function(e) {
      var brawlList = document.getElementById("brawlerSelect1");
      var brawlerId = brawlList.options[brawlList.selectedIndex].value;

      var shareUrl = 'https://share.brawlify.com/player/YJRQ0Y8R9%brawlerId'.replace('%brawlerId',((brawlerId=='default')?'':'/'+brawlerId));
      var profileShareImg1 = document.getElementById('profileShareImg1');
      if (profileShareImg1) {
        profileShareImg1.src = shareUrl;
        profileShareImg1.onload = function() {
          var fb = document.getElementById('shareImage1-FB');
          if (fb) {
            fb.href="https://www.facebook.com/sharer/sharer.php?u="+encodeURIComponent(shareUrl.split("?")[0]);
          }
          var rt = document.getElementById('shareImage1-RT');
          if (rt) {
            rt.href="https://www.reddit.com/submit?url="+encodeURIComponent(shareUrl.split("?")[0])+"&title="+encodeURIComponent("Check out ivankachan\'s profile!");
          }
          var tw = document.getElementById('shareImage1-TW');
          if (tw) {
            tw.href="https://twitter.com/intent/tweet?source="+encodeURIComponent(shareUrl.split("?")[0])+"&text="+encodeURIComponent("Check out ivankachan\'s profile!\n\n"+shareUrl.split("?")[0]);
          }
        }
      }
  });

  // Support for copying to clipboard for giveaways on twitter
  function fallbackCopyTextToClipboard(text) {
    var textArea = document.createElement("textarea");
    textArea.value = text;
    textArea.style.top = "0";
    textArea.style.left = "0";
    textArea.style.position = "fixed";
    document.body.appendChild(textArea);
    textArea.focus();
    textArea.select();
    try {
      var successful = document.execCommand('copy');
      var msg = successful ? 'successful' : 'unsuccessful';
      console.log('Fallback: Copying text command was ' + msg);
    } catch (err) {
      console.error('Fallback: Oops, unable to copy', err);
    }
    document.body.removeChild(textArea);
  }
  function copyTextToClipboard(text) {
    if (!navigator.clipboard) {
      fallbackCopyTextToClipboard(text);
      return;
    }
    navigator.clipboard.writeText(text).then(function() {
      console.log('Async: Copying to clipboard was successful!');
    }, function(err) {
      console.error('Async: Could not copy text: ', err);
    });
  }

  function setCookieBackup(cname, cvalue, exdays) {
    let d = new Date();
    d.setTime(d.getTime() + (exdays * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000));
    let expires = "expires="+d.toUTCString();
    document.cookie = cname + "=" + cvalue + ";" + expires + ";path=/";
  }

  function verifyPremiumEmail(email) {
    //if (!/^\w+@[a-zA-Z_]+?\.[a-zA-Z]{2,20}$/.test(email)) return alert('Invalid email format provided! â›”\n\nIf this isn\'t your profile page, make sure you visit your profile page or try again.');
    var xhr = new XMLHttpRequest();
    xhr.open('POST', 'https://api.brawlify.com/v1/subscriptions/'+playerTag.replace('#',''), true);
    xhr.timeout = 15000;
    xhr.send(JSON.stringify({email:email}));
    xhr.onreadystatechange = processRequest;
    function processRequest(e) {
        if (xhr.readyState == 4) {
            if (xhr.status == 200) {
              if (setCookie) setCookie("premiumUser", playerTag.replace('#',''), 30);
              else if (setCookieBackup) setCookieBackup("premiumUser", playerTag.replace('#',''), 30);
              alert('Successfully verified your email! âœ…\n\nWe will now refresh this page, enjoy your ad-free browsing.\nThank you for supporting us!');
              return location.reload();
            } else if (xhr.status == 403) {
              alert('Invalid email address provided! â›”\n\nIf this isn\'t your profile, make sure you visit your profile page or try again.');
            } else {
              alert('Something went wrong on our side, please try again later!\n\nThere may have been a connection issue.');
            }
        }
    }
  }
